Ang sabi daw ng iba..

 

Nakakamatay ang mga test..

 

Totoo naman kung hindi ka mag-aaral..

 

Nangyayari lamang ang mga ganito kapag magtatapos na ang Quarter..

 

Pero...

 

Kung ang mga test na ito ay mismong nakakamatay nga..

 

Anong gagawin mo?

 

Sasagutin nyo ba sabay sabay?

 

O

 

Sasagutin mo lang ng mag-isa.

 

Tapos man o hindi, kailangan sagutin..

 

Dahil kung hindi..

 

Katapusan mo na..

 

One single question can reveal your true nature..

 

Timer start's now..

####################################
1. New Classmate
####################################


"Okay Class, may bago kayong kaklase, I want you to meet, JC, bago lang sya sa school so be nice to him." Sabi ng isang Highschool teacher na babae na si Ma'am Amy. Lumitaw ang isang lalaking mga nasa edad na 16, maputi ang katawan at katamtaman ang katawan, gwapo pero, mahiyain, sya si JC.

"Uhmm, G-good morning po sa inyo, sana po, maging kaibigan ko po kayo." Pero, parang walang tao ang may pakielam sa binata kaya, mas lalo pa syang nahiya. Bakit pa ako kasi pumasok sa class na ito. Sabi sa kanyang sarili sa utak, tinuro sa kanya ni Ma'am Amy ang upuan nya at doon sya sa dulo na ang gilid nito ay bintana. "Okay Class, turn your book to page 98." At nagsimula nang magklase ang guro, kinuha ni JC ang kanyang notebook at hindi sya makatingin ng diretso sa harapan nya dahil nahihiya sya. biglang bumukas yung pinto at nagpakita ang isang magandang dalaga.

"Sorry po ma'am kung late ako!!! Napunta po ako sa maling jeep kaya na late po ako."

"That's okay Sydney, now, sit beside with JC."

"Ma'am, sino po si JC?"

"Nakikita mo ba yung lalaking iyon? Katabi mo na sya ngayon."

Kinuha nya yung bag nya at tumabi sa isang upuan na katabi nya si JC. Nagpatuloy si Amy sa pagtuturo until kailangan nila ng papel para masagutan nila ang Quiz. Walang papel si Sydney, nanghingi sya sa iba nyang kaklase pero hindi sya pinapansin dahil may pagka immature ang kanyang personality until nakita nya si JC na may papel.

"Uhmm, K-kuya, pwede pong... Manghingi ng papel?" Pinunit ni JC ang isang buong papel at binigay kay Sydney. "Salamat po, teka, ano po ba ulit ang pangalan nyo?" Tanong ni Sydney habang sumasagot si JC ng test.

"JC, JC De Vera ang pangalan ko."

"Ahh, ako nga pala si Sydney de Rochefort, it was nice meeting you." Pero hindi sumagot si JC dahil naging busy sya sa pagsagot ng seatwork, nag deep sigh na lang si Sydney at sinagutan na lang ang seatwork.

-------------- 5 Minutes Later -----------------

"Okay Class, na check ko na yung papers nyo and... Ang highest score natin ay 47 out of 50 at kilala nyo ba kung sino iyon?" Sabi ni Ma'am Amy ng nakangiti habang hawak hawak nya yung papel na may 47 Out of 50, yung mga ibang kaklase, tinutukoy nila yung top 1 nilang si Isaiah, at si Isaiah naman, nagyayabang dahil sa tingin nya, sya yung taong tinutukoy ni Ma'am Amy.

"That is JC De Vera!!!" Nagulat ang buong klase including Isaiah, ang daming bulungan na imposible na matalo ni JC ang isang Top 1 na may Average na 91.30%, pati rin si Sydney ay namangha kay JC, biglang tumunog yung bell at ibig sabihin nun ay recess na, umalis na yung buong klase at naiwan na lang si JC, kinuha nya lang yung bag nya at pumunta sa hallway na may locker, he opened the lock at......

Biglang nahulog ang mga libro at pencil nya, nagtawanan ang mga estudyante na nakakita sa pangyayari, kinuha ni JC ang mga gamit nya at nilagay ulit sa locker, nahihiya na tuloy sya lalo, hindi lang sa pinagtatawanan sya, kundi na rin sa bad impression sa kanya, he took again his backpack and naglakad na lang as if nothing had happened.

--------- Classroom -------------

"Class, magkakaroon tayo ng 2 Weeks Examination para sa college nyo, para pagdating ng mga Entrance Exam sa bawat eskuwelahan na papasukan nyo, it will be just a piece of cake, do you understand me?" Sabi ng isang principal sa classroom ni JC, all the students looked like their being punished through their bad deeds habang si JC nakayuko lang at pinapakinggan ang sinasabi ng guro, napatingin sa kanya si Sydney at naging malungkot ang itsura nya sa kanya.

"JC, may nangyari ba sa iyo?"

Hindi sya sumagot at nakayuko pa rin sya. 

"Pero, ang mga estudyante na magkakaroon ng 2 Week Examination at yun ang  mga Top 25 na Students." Nakaramdam naman ng relief ang mga estudyanteng hindi kasali sa Top 25, yung mga Top Notchers naman, parang 'pamatay' na sa kanila ang 2 Week Examination, kasama kasi si JC sa Top Notchers bilang Top 2 pero, wala na syang pake doon, nang marinig nila yung last bell, nag uwian na yung mga ibang estudyante, nag iimpake pa lang si JC ng biglang nilapitan sya ni Sydney.

"JC, pwede ka ba sumabay sa akin pag uwi?"

"I don't know, may gagawin pa ako ehh.

"Come on, para may kasama ka naman."

Hindi naman pwedeng tumanggi si JC kaya pumayag na lang sya, naglalakad sila ngayon sa isang sunset atmosphered na kalye. "So JC, may pamilya ka ba?"

"Wala, iniwan ko ang sarili kong magulang sa States."

"Ibig sabihin, layas ka?"

"Oo, they always force me to do things like this, like that , I'm done with those things kaya, tumakas ako sa states at tumira sa pilipinas ng sarili kong pagsisikap."

"I see, well, may bahay ka ba?"

"Wala akong bahay, umuupa lang ako sa condo kaya... Nabubuhay akong mag isa doon."

Tumingin sa lapag si Sydney habang naglalakad. "Well... Y-you can stay sa house ko today."

"Ano?"

"I'm just telling you na palagi kang welcome sa bahay ko."

"Why are you telling me like this?"

" Cause..... I want to know more about you."

Tumigil sa paglalakad si JC at ganun din si Sydney. " So... Ano maiisip mo?"

"Pag-iisipan ko muna." Sabi nya at naglakad na sya, tinatawag sya ni Sydney pero hindi nya ito pinapansin.

------------ Room 1189 -------------

Pagpasok sa kwarto ni JC, nilagay nya yung bag nya sa higaan at hinubad ang kanyang uniform, sinuot ang kanyang pambahay na damit, at umupo sa isang upuan na ang harapan nya ay isang salamin, naalala tuloy ni JC yung buhay nya sa States pero, ayaw nya nang maalala iyon.

"Musta JC, It's been a long time."

To Be Continued.....

####################################
2. Jack The Reaper and Becky The Doll
####################################


"Musta JC, it's been a long time." Lumingon si JC sa likod nya at nakita nya ang kanyang magandang ate na si Vanessa, sa buong pamilya ni JC, kay Vanessa lang sya sumusunod, nakikinig at nakikipag-usap, biglang tumulo ang mga luha ni JC at niyakap ang kanyang ate. "Ate, akala ko, iiwanan mo na ako."

"Bakit pa ba kita iiwan, diba, ang sabi ko sa iyo, palagi tayong magkasama."

Nakaramdam ng saya at ginhawa ng makayap nya si Vanessa ng biglang nakaramdam sya ng isang basa mula sa likod ng kanyang ate, pagtingin nya sa kamay nya, may dugo, biglang nag iba ang ihip ng hangin, tumataas ang kanyang balahibo, yung shape ng kamay ng kanyang ate, parang iba. Hindi si Vanessa ang kanyang niyayakap, kundi, isang nilalang na hindi nya dapat makita, slowly na tumanggal sa pagyayakap si JC ng biglang nakita nya ang mukha ng kanyang ate, pula ang mga mata nya, may mga ugat ito sa mukha nya, may dugo pa sa kanyang damit, ngumiti ng nakakatakot ang ate sa kanya.

"Tulungan mo ko." Biglang lumapit sa kanya si Vanessa ng biglang nagising si JC sa panaginip, paano..... Bakit nakita ko si Ate Vanessa? Sabi sa kanyang sarili, natulog na lang sya ulit sa kanyang higaan at sana, hindi na maulit muli ang kanyang napanaginipan.

---------- Classroom ------------

"Class, Next week na magsisimula ang 2 week examination at may isang week na lang kayo para mag review, mag iistart ang examination from 7 AM to 8 PM." Mas lalong naging tamad at naiinis ang mga mukha ng iba't ibang estudyante, tumingin si Sydney kay JC at nakatingin lang ito sa bintana, nakaramdam naman ng kilig si Sydney dahil ang cute nya daw tignan kapag nakatingin lang sya sa bintana, tumingin sa kanya si JC at mabilis naman nakaiwas ng tingin si Sydney, tumingin ulit si JC sa bintana ng biglang tumunog yung bell, kinuha nya na lang yung bag nya at umalis sa classroom papuntang canteen ng biglang hinablot sya ng limang tao papunta sa isang abandonadong classroom. Nakita nya si Isaiah, ang kanyang karibal na Top Notcher.

"Well, well, well, it's the newbie guy who took away my reputation." Bigla naman nagtawanan yung kasama nitong mga kaibigan.

"Oh my gosh, look at him, he look scared, aww, wag kang matakot, di ka namin sasaktan." Sabay tumawa ang dalaga. "Ayy Danica, wag mo pa sya lalong takutin, nanginginig na nga sa takot, tatakutin mo pa?" Sabay tawa, So, pangalan pala ng babaeng iyan ay Danica. Sabi sa kanyang sarili.

"A-anong gagawin ninyo sa akin?"

"Wag kang pumasok bukas."

"Bakit? Ano ba ang ginawa ko sa iyo?"


"Let's just say na.... You are a threat to me."

"Threat ako... Sa'yo?"

"Oo, simula nung sinagutan mo yung quiz, I can't believe you got 47 out of 50, siguro... May kodigo ka no?"

"Wala akong kodigo, nasagutan ko yun dahil mahilig akong mag-aral."

"Aba, hindi ka lang ugly guy, nerdy ka pa!!!" Sabay tumawa silang lima, halos, papatak na yung luha ni JC sa kanyang mga mata pero, hindi nya iyon ilalabas sa harapan nila. "Ano?/ Iiyak ka ba? Wag kang mag-alala, di ka iiyak kapag hindi ka pumasok bukas, pero... Kapag pumasok ka.. Baka.. Pagsisisihan mo ang ginawa mo sa pagpasok sa eskuwelahan na ito, enjoy studying." Sabay kinuha ni Isaiah ang bag ni JC at tinapon sa isang sulok ng classroom at iniwanan sya na magisa sa abandonadong Classroom, kukunin nya sana yung kanyang bag ng biglang may tumatawag sa kanyang pangalan, pagtalikod nya, isang lalaki na nakasuot na black leather jacket, di nya makita yung mukha dahil isa lang yung bumbilya.

"JC ba ang pangalan mo?"

Nakaramdam sya tuloy ng takot dahil yung tono ng pagkasabi sa kanya ang nagbigay ng pagtaas ng kanyang mga balahibo, kumuha sya ng isang upuan at umupo sya na nakaharap kay JC pero di nya makita yung mukha. "Anong k-kailangan mo s-sa akin?"

"Ikaw.... Ikaw ang kailangan ko."

"What do you mean?"

Biglang lumabas ang isang babae na may maikiling palda, naka black leather din pero, hindi makita ang mukha dahil isa lang ang bumbilya sa abandonadong klase na ito. "We know about your sister's death." Nagulat doon si JC, di sya makgalaw dahil, pa-paano nila nalaman ang pagkamatay ng ate nya, tanong sa kanyang sarili. "I don't know what you are talking about at kung ano man ito, hinding hindi ako sasali."

"It's that so JC? Sayang naman kung hindi mo mabibigyan ng hustisya ang ate mo." Sabi ng isang lalaki habang nakaupo parin sya sa upuan, katabi nya ay yung isang babae. "ANO BA KASI ANG KAILANGAN NYO SA AKIN?? WALA NAMAN AKONG GINAWANG MASAMA SA INYO AH!!!"

"We know that, wala ka ngang ginawang masama sa amin pero... May plano kami para sa iyo."

"Ano ang plano nyo?"

Lumapit ng few meters ang babae at huminto rin sya para hindi makita ni JC ang mga mukha nila. "We are planning revenge.... Di mo ba alam, ang ate mo ay parang kapatid na namin, she is always there kapag kailangan namin sya, she always talks about you and, kaming dalawa ay naging interested sa iyo, sabi nya sa amin, sasamahan nya raw kami papunta sa bahay nyo at makikipaglaro tayo pero... Di na yun dumating.. Dahil natagpuan syang patay sa isang bakuran ng isang abandonadong bahay." Biglang umiyak yung dalagita at bumalik sa lalake, dahil dim ang lights, alam ni JC na pinapatahan ng lalaki yung babae sa pag iyak, nang tumigil na sya, lumapit sya kay JC ng few meters at inabot ang kamay.

"Come my brother.... We can avenge your sister's death, actually, kaklase mo ang mga murderers na iyon, if you cooperate with our 'Periodical Exam', we can avenge your sister's death." Nagdadalawang isip si JC, gusto nyang bigyan ng hustisya ang kanyang ate dahil, hindi nahanap ng pulis ang mga suspek dahil kulang sila sa ebidensya, kaya, namatay sya ng hindi nahuhuli ang suspek, secondly, masama ang gagawin nya, makakapatay sya ng tao dahil sa galit at hirap na dinanas nya sa loob ng 3 taon, aabutin nya sana yung kamay ng bigla nyang hininto yung kanyang kamay.

"Anong meron, kapatid?"

"I... I think... I think I'm not ready for this.." Binalik ng lalaki ulit ang kanyang kamay at nakita ni JC ang bibig nito na nakangiti ng demonyo. "Okay... We will give you 3 days to think about this, pag hindi ka sumali, makakasali ka sa aming 'Periodical Test' pero, kung sumli ka, ligtas ka pero.. Matututo kang pumatay ng tao." Aalis sila ng biglang tinawag nya yung lalaki at yung babae.

"A-ano ba muna ang pangalan nyo?"

Biglang namatay yung ilaw, kaya walang makita si JC pero, may flashlight sya sa kanyang bag pero, di nya makita yung bag. "Gusto mo ba malaman ang mga pangalan namin?"

"G-gusto kong malaman."

"Okay... Ako nga pala si Jack The Reaper, at ito naman ang aking kapatid na si Becky The Doll, at kami ang inyong Death Reapers, we're gonna send them to hell... Remember that, JC De Vera." At tumawa ng evil ang dalawa at maya maya, nawala na yung tunog, hinahanap ni JC ang kanyang bag ng biglang bumukas yung pintuan, binuksan ng isang dalagang babae ang isang bumbilya at nakita ni JC si Sydney.

"What the heck JC? Hinahanap kita for like 2 Hours and dito ka lang pala, you make me so worried, anong ginagawa mo dito?"

"Nabully kasi ako ng mga ka-tropa ni Isaiah kaya napunta ako dito."

"Mga bullies na iyan... Oh sige, punta na kaagad na tayo sa classroom at may gagawin pa tayong assignment." Kinuha ni JC ang kanyang bag at umalis sa abandonadong classroom, biglang pumasok sa utak ni JC si Jack The Reaper at si Becky The Doll... Sino ba sila? At ano nga ba ang kailangan nila kay JC?

(To Be Continued)
####################################
3. Memento Mori
####################################


Nag uuwian na ang mga ibang estudyante except kay Sydney at kay JC dahil cleaners sila, pagkatapos nilang maglinis, naisipan ni JC na bumisita lang kahit saglit sa bahay ni Sydney.

"Ano... Sydney, pwede bang bumisita sa inyo?"

"Hah? Bakit mo nasabi yan?"

"Kasi..... Naisipan ko lang." Nag isip muna si Sydney bago sumagot ng oo, ngumiti naman si JC sa kanya, kinuha na ang kanilang bag at sabay ni lock ang pintuan ng kanilang room, paglabas nila sa school, nakatanggap ng phone call si JC mula sa isang unknown call. "hello?"

"Memento Mori..."

"Hello?? Ano po ba yung sinasabi nyo? Hello??" Sabay pinatay ni JC ang kanyang phone, hindi masyado naintindihan ni JC yung sinabi pero, narinig nya ang salitang Memento Mori. "Sino yung kausap mo sa cellphone?"

"Wala, isang unknown call lang mula sa isang unknown caller." Nagpatuloy lang sila sa paglalakad ng makarating na sila sa loob ng bahay ni Sydney, nilapag nya yung bag nya sa sofa  habang si JC ay buhat buhat nya parin. "Alam mo, pwede mong ilagay mo yung bag mo doon sa sofa, wag ka nang mahiya, sige, ilagay mo na." Nilagay ni JC ang bag nya sa sofa at umupo, tiningnan nya ang buong bahay ni Sydney, simple lang, may mga picture frames ni Sydney kasama ang kanyang magulang at mga kapatid.

"Ito oh JC, inom ka muna ng juice." Kinuha ni JC yung juice at ininom. "So JC, anong buhay mo sa states?" Napatigil naman sa pag inom si JC at nilapag nya yung baso nya sa lamesa. "mahirap.... Mahirap ang buhay ko doon, mayaman kasi ang pamilya namin doon sa States, they always think their business instead of their own kids, ang panganay sa pamilya namin ay si Ate Vanessa at kasunod ako. My parents have a big expectation kay ate pero... Nung namatay sya at natagpuang patay sa isang abandonadong bahay, iyak ng iyak ang nanay ko at ako... Di ako makapaniwala sa nangyari nun, kinukulong ko sarili ko sa kwarto ko at umiiyak, ngayon, yung expectation nila kay ate, napunta sa akin... Babantayin talaga nila ang lahat ng maling gawa ko and they will correct me."

"So... Anong ginawa mo?"

"I left them, habang natutulog sila, kinuh ko yung mga gamit ko at tumakas mula sa bintana, kinuha ko yung passport ko at pumunta sa pilipinas, aaminin ko na pagbagsak ko pa lang sa lup ng pilipinas, mahirap nang mamuhay kaya, heto ako ngayon, isang normal boy na nakatira sa isang inuupahan na condo."

"So.... Do you think your parents keep looking for you?"

"Naiisip ko yun pero.... I don't care about them anymore, sa lahat ng taong minahal ko, si Ate Vanessa lang... Di ko alam bakit sya namatay..... Dahil ba sa magulang ko? Kasi, yung trato yata nila kay ate, napupunta sa akin.... Maybe she comitted suicide.. Or maybe.... Someone killed her?" Biglang tumigil sa pagsasalita si JC dahil naalala nya ang sinabi ng isang unknown caller sa kanya, ang Memento Mori..

"Sydney... Alam mo ba yung salitang Memento Mori?"

"Yeah, palagi ko yun naririnig lalo kapag death anniversary sa isang taong namatay." Nanlaki ang mga mata ni JC dahil, pagtingin nya pa lang sa kalendaryo ni Sydney, nalaman nyang death anniversary pala ng kanyang ate..  January 18, 2009 or 1/18/09. Biglang naalala ni JC ang room number nya sa condo... 1189... "JC, okay ka lang ba?"

"H-ha? Oo, okay lang ako, tell me... What does Memento Mori means?"

"Memento Mori, naririnig mo itong salitang ito lalo na sa mga Death Anniversary ng isang taong namatay, the meaning of Memento Mori is Remember your Mortality o, Remember your Death. It means, every people die in a very unexpected way, for example, namatay ang isang tao dahil nalason sya, nasagasaan, it depends doon sa situation."

"Kanino nanggaling yung salitang Memento Mori?"

"Ano, walang explaination dyan pero, according doon sa history book namin, na discover ang word na Memento Mori sa isang Roman general na nagpa-parade doon sa streets ng biglang nakita nya ang salitang Memento Mori, at dahil dun, he told his expert manghuhula what is the meaning of Memento Mori, it said, remember that you will die..."

"So..."

"Tapos... yung symbol ng Memento Mori na ito, ay yung bungo ng isang tao pero, dahil 21st Century ang ating generation, people called that bone, Death Reaper.

Reaper.... Ang salitang pumasok sa isip ni JC, biglang pumasok sa isip nya ang pangalan ni Jack The Reaper, sino ba yung unknown caller na iyan na nagsabi na Memento Mori mismo sa Death Anniversary ng kanyang ate at bakit Memento Mori ang kanyang sinabi? Yan ang mahahalagang tanong na bawal kalimutan ni JC, nagpaalam na sya kay Sydney at umuwi na, habang naglalakad sya sa madilim na kalye, bigla syang napahinto dahil isang vision ang pumasok sa mga mata ni JC.

1. A Girl smiling in front of him.

2. 1189, no. ng kanyang condo.

3. 5 Fingers, one by one, natatanggal.

4. dalawang bungo na may hawak na isang Scythe.

at ang huli, ang eskuwelahan ni JC. He shooked his head again at naglakad na lang papunta sa condo nya, pagpasok nya sa loob, kinuha nya kaagad ang laptop nya at sinearch ang salitang Memento Mori at magkatugma nga ito sa sinabi ni Sydney pangalawa, he searches about Death Reaper, he was also known as Angel of Death, he is responsible for the people's death at depende na iyon sa situation ng isang tao. at last, he searches about Death Test, kinlick na ang isang website at naging black yung background nito at isang bungo ang lumabas, pagkatapos nun, isang kakaibang website ang lumabas.

 He clicked the meaning of Death Test. It is a kind of test for the people who committed something wrong especially killing, Death Test literally occur when Death tries to test the people, occasionally, 25 people are taking this test and once they answer the test incorrectly, one by one, these 25 people are going to die, depending on its environment. Kinalibutan doon si JC, then, he scrolled down at lumabas ang isang kind of date. 

1. February 24 1568 - Death gave these 25 people in a small school of Mexico a death test and, police said, only five people died and the other 25 escaped, witnesses said that they heard a scary voice then, it started killing people through puzzles, if you answered it wrong, that person is going to die.

2. March 1, 1616 - 25 People died in a fire in a private school at Cuba, police said, they have died in a severe electricution and result death.

3. August 28 1967 - 25 people trapped in a public school just after their Periodical Test at Washington DC, 5 people reported killed, student said, these 5 people died in a very mysterious way, some said they died because they answered the test wrong, some say, they are killed accidentally because of these 'puzzle'.

Tumigil sa pag re-research si JC dahil natatakot n sya at pinagpapawisan, tumingin muna sya sa bintana at, may nakita syang dalawang tao na nakatingin sa kanya, isang lalaking my bungong mukha at isang babae na may manikang mukha na nakangiti. Nag scrub ng mata si JC at biglang nawala yung dalawang tao, he immediately locked his door, napahiga na lang sya sa kanyang higaan..

Memento Mori... Death.... Death Test..... Ano ba ang dahilan kung bakit may ganyan?

####################################
4. Bullying Kills
####################################


Nagising si JC sa kanyang alarm clock, it's already 7:30 AM, biglang pumasok sa isip nya ang threat na binigay sa kanya ni Isaiah, kapag pumasok sya ngayon, may mangyayaring masama sa kanya, di alam ni JC kung ano ang gagawin nya, pumasok ba o wag pumasok?? Yan ngayon ang numero uno nyang problema, maya maya, biglang tumunog ang cellphone nya, kinuha nya kaagad ito at naka receive sya ng call mula kay Sydney.

"hello?"

"Good Morning JC, ano, intayin kita s gate, wala kasi akong kasabay pumasok sa room ehh."

"Bakit? May kaibigan ka naman na makakasabay mo pagpasok sa room."

"Ehh, gusto ko ikaw ehh!!! Ayoko na sa mga kaibigan ko, they always back stab me you know, alam mo ba, ikaw lng yung totoong kaibigan ko?? Ayy sorry, anong oras na ba? Maligo ka na at iintayin pa kita sa gate, sige na bye bye!!!"

At biglang pinatay ni Sydney yung call, napangiti si JC dahil, first time nya lang matawagan ng isang babae, naligo na sya at sinuot ang kanyang uniform, pagdating nya sa gate ng school nila, nandoon si Sydney, naghihintay, nakita sya kaagad at lumapit si Sydney kay JC.

"Well, ang aga mo ngayon ahhh, anyway, may quiz daw tayo, kaya maaga tayo, so, let's go!!" Biglang hinila ni Sydney ang kamay ni JC papunta sa room nya, pagpasok nya palang sa classroom, ang una nyang hinanap, si Isaiah at... Nahuli sya, nakaramdam ng takot si JC kay Isaiah, nakangiti ito ng demonyo sa kanya, pumunta na lang sya sa kanyang upuan ng biglang dumating si Ma'am Amy. "Okay class, may quiz tayo ngayon and, I expect na may isang tao ang magkakaroon ng high score, sana, don't let me down kung sino man yun." Then, she started giving the students a question paper, habang sumasagot si JC ng quiz, isang papel ang tumama sa kanyang answer sheet, isang lukot na bilog na papel, he unwrapped the paper and saw a threat.

January 16, 2013...

Ano ba yan, na late kasi ako kanina ehh, paano kasi, ang traffic sa Edsa tapos nag flat yun gulong ng jeep, kainis argh... Pero, may nakita akong bagong classmate, at ang gwapo nya KYAAAHHH!!! Biglang tinutok nya sa mukha ni JC pero nahawakan ito ni JC, pinipilit ni Matt na saksakin sya sa mukha pero, di nya magawa dahil hinawakan sya ni JC, maya maya, tinamaan ni JC ang bandang parte sa puson, sumigaw sa sakit si Matt, nakaalis sya kay Matt, JC quickly tooked the gun pero, pumunta kaagad si Matt kay Isaiah, he holded his head up at tinutok ang kanyang kutsilyo sa leeg ni Isaiah.

"Oh, don't point your gun at me, if you killed me, mamamatay rin si Isaiah.... Now JC, for the final test, I swear to God, kahit isang bala ang lumabas sa baril na iyan, I'm sure na mamamatay itong binata na ito, pero, if you put the gun on the floor and let me kill you.. I will spare his life." Napatingin si JC kay Isaiah. "N-no JC, kill him.."

"Pero Isaiah, if I do that, you're going to die."

"D-don't worry about me... I'll be okay." Napaluha si JC, he is now making a difficult descision. "Aww JC, you know, making a difficult descision is easy, either sacrifice your friend to kill me or... Sacrifice your life to me and I will spare him." Napatingin sya ulit kay Isaiah, he slowly put his hands on the air and nilaglag ang baril, ngumit ng demonyo si Matt, tinanggal nya sa leeg ang kutsilyo at lumapit kay JC pero... Bago pa sya makalapit, mabilis na napahiga si JC sa lapag, kinuha ni JC ang baril at tinamaan nya ito sa paa, nadapa sa lapag si Matt at hinahawakan nya ang parte na natamaan ni JC.

"W-why did you shoot me?"

"Bakit, di ba obvious? You killed Danica.." Tinamaan nya ito sa balikat. "You killed my teacher Amy." Binaril nya ito sa tiyan. "And you killed my my friend Sydney, you're going to pay to what you did to them." Tinutok ni JC ang baril sa ulo ni Matt... Maya maya...

 

 

Pinaputok nya ito, hindi pa sya nakuntento, he kept on hitting and killing him, every part of his body, his eyes were like hunger for killing, his smile, he is smiling like he is enjoying it, nakita ni Isaiah ang ibang 'JC' ang nakikita nya sa harapan nya, nang maubos na ang lahat ng bala, he simply throwed the gun at tumingin kay Isaiah, hanggang ngayon, di pa nya alam kung paano ba makakaalis si Isaiah sa debris, biglang dumating ang mga rescue team, at tumakbo papalapit kay JC at kay Isaiah, buti na lang, natanggal ng mga rescue team ang debris at nakaligtas sa peligro sina JC at Isaiah.

------ Outside of the Gym ------

Sa labas ng gym, nandoon lahat ang mga sasakyan ng ambulansya, pulis at may ilang reporters dito na sinasabi ang ganitong sitwasyon, nakasakay sa loob si JC, Ella at Isaiah na nakahiga sa higaan.. Sa wakas, tapos na rin ang mga test na ito.....

 

------ Hospital ------

Habang nagpapahinga si Isaiah, napatingin si JC sa kanyang madugong kamay, naramdaman nya ang galit at saya nang mapatay nya si Matt, hindi nya na kilala kung sino ba talaga sya... Nang makapasok na ang doctor at si Ella, nagising si Isaiah, the doctor said he is in fine condition, mild lang ang fracture ng bones nya, nang makaalis ang doctor, lumapit si JC kay Ella at kay Isaiah.

"Guys.... I have to go away." 

"Ano?" Sabay na pagkasabi ni Ella at ni Isaiah. "I have to go back to the states."

"Pero bakit?" Tanong sa kanya ni Isaiah. "I have to return where I belong... Sa states, I have to take care something doon... I have to escape this nightmare.... Don't worry, mamimiss ko kayo, I'll be back.... As soon as I can.." Napaiyak si Ella kaya niyakap nya si JC, nakipag apir sa kanya si Isaiah.

"You know JC, pinagsisisihan ko na bullihin ka.... Kung wala ka sa school namin, baka matagal na kaming patay, you saved our lives JC, and we're happy that we're still alive." Napangiti si JC, binuksan nya na yung pintuan, he stared at them for like 5 seconds at umalis na sya sa room ni Isaiah.

To Be Continued....

22. Going Back Where I Belong
####################################


2 Years Later...

"There has been a similar cases between Frayville National Highschool and Oscar Academy that has a mass killing that contains 'puzzle' and 'test', criminologist said 'this is a new way of killing and this is the worst of the worst cases that has ever invented', students who survived the incident said 'in order to escape those test, they must answer the puzzle and save the victims.' This is Carmella, reporting live from CBS news." Nanonood ng t.v si JC, nasa states na sya ngayon.

"Sir, hinahanap po kayo ng inyong bisita." Sabi ng kanyang secretary. "At... Sino yun?"

"It's about the SteelAsia Company.."

"They're going to brag a money again huh? Well, cancel the meeting, I'm going back to the Philippines."

"Pero sir, sino mag ha-handle ng kompanya."

"It's very obvious, my parents." Then lumabas na sya sa office at pumasok sa loob ng kanyang sasakyan, he is now the Boss of the famous steel company named Reglar Steel, habang nag da-drive sya, he opened the radio at pinaguusapan parin ang case ng Frayville Academy... He doesn't want to remember any of it, gusto nya nang makalimutan ang nangyari.... "The students.... The psychopaths..." Bulong sa kanyang sarili... Nang makarating na sya sa bahay nya, pumasok sya sa loob at umupo muna sa sofa.

Binuklat nya ang dyaryo at nakita nya ang case ng FrayVille, pumikit sya muna ng sandali at pumasok sa isip nya ang nangyari sa gym.... Still, di parin sya makaalis sa nightmare na iyon, yung ginawa nya kay Matt ay isang bangungot sa sarili nya, pagkadilat nya, dumating ang kanyang butler na si Sebastian.

"Sir.... Ba't po kayo nandirito?"

"Pack my things."

"I'm sorry sir?"

"I said, pack my things, I'm going back to the Philippines." Pumunta si Sebastian sa kanyang kwarto at inayos ang kanyang mga damit at gamit, habang nakaupo sa sofa si JC, biglang dumating ang kanyang mga magulang. Nagulat ang kanyang nanay dahil nandito sya.

"My goodness, JC, ba't wala ka sa opisina?" Pero, di sya sumagot. "JC DE VERA, BA'T DI KA PUMASOK SA OPISINA?"

"Pumasok ako.... Tinatamad lang ako." Bumaba si Sebastian na may dalang baggage ni JC. "Saan ka pupunta?"

"I'm going back to the Philippines."

"NO... You are not going anywhere unless you finish your job."

"I can finish it whatever I want."

"God, JC, ano ba ang nangyayari sa iyo? What would happen to us if our moey is lost? What if-"

"So here we are, talking about money again, mama, palagi nyo na lang iniisip ang pera, walang iba kundi business, pera, pera business, nung sinundo nyo ko sa Pilipinas, wala man lang kayon alala sa akin, I have experienced a bad thing sa school na iyon ma, and now, ito na naman ha?"

"Why are you being like that to your mom?"

"Tsk, siguro ito yung dahilan kung bakit namatay ang aking ate."

"Stop it JC."

"No ma.... Think about it, kung ano ang trato nyo sa akin siguro ganito rin yung trato nyo sa kanya? No wonder she died... Excuse me dahil may pupuntahan akong.... Business vacation. Sebastian, let's go." Iniwan ni JC na speechless ang kanyang nanay, sumakay na sya sa sasakyan kasama si Sebastian, JC is now a grown up man, he is now 21 yrs. old, mature and confident to himself, ibang iba na sya sa sarili nya dati noong nasa pilipinas pa sya, when he reached the airport, umupo sya sa kanyang seat sa eroplano at natulog muli.

 

He woke up at napansin nya na wala ang mga tao sa loob ng eroplano, maya maya, biglang tumunog ang kanta ni Beethoven na Fur Elise then... May nagsalita sa speaker. "Now, for the final test.... Either kill me or kill yourself." Pagtingin nya sa salamin, nakita nya ang pugot na ulo ni Isaiah pero, nagising sya ulit, nasa eroplano parin sya na may tao, yung music sa speaker ay yung Fur Elise ni Beethoven.

"Memorable song.." Sabi nya, nang makalanding na ang eroplano sa airport, he quickly took his bag at pumunta sa bagong condo, his new room is 1213, he got inside the room at.... Malawak ito... Tumingin sya sa parteng may bintana at tumingin sa labas, binuksan nya ang kanyang briefcase at kinuha nya ang picture ng kanyang ate.... Kasama ang mga kaibigan nito, si Isaiah, Matt at Alaina... Lumabas sya ulit sa condo at sumakay sa kanyang sasakyan, habang nagda-drive sya, he came to the Funeral...

Biglang umulan, buti na lang may payong sya, kinuha nya yung dalawang bulaklak at naglakad papasok sa Funeral, while he was walking, nakita nya na ang gravestone ni Sydney.. "Hi there Sydney... It's me, JC." Nilapag nya yung bulaklak sa gravestone nya. "I became a boss sa famous company... Kung tatanungin mo ko kung kamusta na ako... I'm fine... I'm perfectly fine... Sana, kung buhay ka pa, sana niligawan na lang kita... I'm sorry if I didn't save you back there, pero... I know that you will forgive me... I love you, Sydney." Tumayo na sya at pumunta naman sa burol ng kanyang ate, nilapag nya yung bulaklak at tinignan ang kanyang burol, he is happy dahil, nasa magandang lugar na ang kanyang ate at... Nabubuhay na sya na masaya doon.

"JC.... Ikaw ba yan?" Tumalikod sya at nakita nya si Isaiah at si Ella. "Isaiah... Ella, kayo ba yan?"

"Yeah bro.. Ako parin to!!" Nakipag apiran sya kay Isaiah at bineso nya naman si Ella. "How are you guys?"

"We're fine... Totally fine.." Sabi ni Ella. "May balita ka ba tungkol sa amin ni Isaiah?"

"What?"

"We're married and of course.... Buntis ako." Nagulat si JC ng marinig nya iyon. "You're kidding, right?"

"Edi tanungin mo sa asawa ko!!" Tapos may binulong si Ella ky JC. "He is really good in bed." Napatawa naman doon si JC s sinabi ni Ella. "Ehh ikaw JC.... Kamusta ka naman?" Tanong sa kanya ni Isaiah.

"Eto pa rin ako... Single, may sarili nang buhay at business.... Always busy sa gawain." 

"Anong ginagawa mo dito?"

"I just came by here.... I want to visit Sydney and Vanessa's grave.... I really love Philippines... By the way.. What happened to our school?"

"Wala na.... Na demolish iyon after 1 year dahil sa trahedyang nangyari... Naging Department Store na lang iyon."

"I see.... Well, it was nice meeting you... And I have to go... I have some other business to discuss."

"Na miss ka talaga namin JC. And, you've changed.."

"Yeah right." Niyakap ni JC si Isaiah at si Ella, he waved at them at umalis na sa Funeral... Nag stop sya sa isang bridge... He was holding the picture of Vanessa and her friends.... Tinignan nya ito ng mabuti at saka tinapon sa ilog... "You know... Death is something that you cannot escape." Tumalikod si JC at nakita nya ang isang lalaki na naka shades... Masyado syang ma porma and he got this spiky black hair.

"Sino ka?"

"I have many names pero.... You can call me Evan."

"What do you want?"

"I'm here to give you some invitation."

"Invitation?"

"You see.... You survived the incident sa FrayVille Academy and I was so happy that you escape... So, ibibigay ko itong calling card sa iyo... If you're interested to join with me, I'll accept you as soon as I can.... See ya!!" He took the calling card at nakasulat doon ang pangalan na Evan pero... Sa ilalim ng underlined words, may nakasulat na Soul Reaper. "Who are you.... Really?"

"You want to know who I am?" He slowly removed his shades at nagulat doon si JC. "My name is Death... And I'm here to accept your revenge...."

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

Sa isang eskuwelahan... Nagaaral ang pinsan ni Sydney na si Tommy Rochefort Williams, he is a special student sa isang special section na tinatawag na SPA, maya maya, nakarinig sila ng kakaibang tugtog at iyon ang Fur Elise, nagiba ang channel ng t.v at napunta ito sa isang babae na may device sa jaw na ito, nagkaroon ng Sound Distortion ang speaker at naglabas ng isang boses na may halong malalim, mahina, matinis at malakas. "From Now on.... You will be taking another test.... This time, it contains Death..."

 

 

To Be Continued....

"Ahh, 5 minutes daw, gumising ka na at maliligo ka pa!!" Tumayo si Alaina sa kanyang higaan, she scrubs her eyes at nakita nya ang kanyang kuya na nakabihis na. "Opo kuya, tatayo na ako." She standed up at bumaba, she ate her breakfast, naligo at nagbihis, nagtawag sila ng jeep at papunta na silang dalawa sa Oscar Academy. "Alaina.... May dala kang gunting, ruler at protactor?" Tanong sa kanya ni Matt.

"Oo kuya, bakit?"

"Shit naman, wala akong dala ehh."

"Yan kasi, puro ka computer at hindi mo na maalala pa ang dapat mong dalhin..."

"Sorry naman Alaina, di ko naman kasi sinasadya ehh."

"Asus..." Nang makarating na silang dalawa sa Oscar Academy, madaming tao ang nagpapasukan.... maya maya, isang lalaki na naka leather jackets at may shades sya, lumapit sya kay Matt at Alaina. "Uhmm, alam nyo ba kung saan yung FrayVille Academy?"

"Uhmm, punta po kayo doon 3 blocks away tapos kaliwa at kanan po kayo at makikita nyo na doon yung FrayVille Academy." Sabi ni Alaina sa kanya. "Ganun ba? Thank you ahh, oh, and... Good luck on your test, it's going to get bloody." Naguluhan ang magkakapatid ng sinabi nya iyon.

"He's a freak guy, halika na, pasok na tayo!!!" Pumasok na silang dalawa sa school at pumunta sa sariling homeroom nila. "Alaina, good luck on your studies ha, kung may problema ka, sabihin mo lang sa big brother mo..."

"Opo kuya." Nagyakapan silang dalawa sa hallway at naghiwalay sila sa hallway, sa sitwasyon ni Alaina, umupo sya kaagad sa kanyang upuan, then, biglang dumating ang 5 babae at tinignan si Alaina na may disgusting. "Oh my gosh, si nerd girl nandito sya!!"

"Freak!!" At nagtawanan naman ang limang babae, nag ring ang bell at nagbalikan sa upuan ang mga estudyante, pumasok ang kanilang teacher at may dala dalang test paper. "Okay class, we're going to take a quiz... At, balita ko, may prom kayo next week?" Nagbulungan ang mga estudyante dahi excited na sila sa prom... Pero, si Alaina lang ang hindi imbitado... The teacher started to distribute the test papers, nang makarating ito sa kamay ni Alaina, she took her ballpen at sinimulang sagutin.

------ 10 Minutes Later -------

"Okay class, tomorrow na natin ito iche-check at may ia-announce din ako tomorrow tungkol sa prom ninyo, you may now take your recess." Tumayo ang ilang estudyante except kay Alaina na nag iimpake pa ng gamit, maya maya, biglang lumapit ang isang babae sa kanya na mataray. "Hey Freak, gusto mo bang ma invite sa prom, then, magpaka ganda ka ahh!!" Then, tumawa lang sya at umalis, she stayed in her chair for like 2 Minutes then, tumayo sya at kinuha ang bag at umalis...

 

Meanwhile, si Matt ay naimbitado sa prom dahil, isa syang famous athlete sa school nila, maraming babae ang nagi-invite sa kanya sa prom pero, may hinihintay sya.... Yung kanyang long time crush na si Alexia ang kanyang hinihintay na imbitahin sya, nag recess na, he took his bag at umalis sa classroom, he was finding her sister Alaina pero, hindi nya makita, wonder where she up to? Biglang lumapit sa kanya ang limang babae at tinapik sya sa likod at tumingin naman si JC sa likod nya at nakita nya kung sino yung tumapik sa kanila.

"Tiffany, what are you doing here?"

"So.... Are you invited to the prom?"

"Oh, hell yeah!!"

"Good.... See you next week!!" then umalis yung mga babae habang kinikilig sila na makita ang isang gwapong, famous athlete sa school nila. Anyway, nasaan kaya yung kanyang kapatid na si Alaina?

 

Naglakad si Alaina papuntang library at doon sya nag-aral ng mga libro, maya maya, pumunta din si Matt sa library at nakita nya ang kanyang kapatid, mabilis naman syang tumabi at nakaharap ang kanyang kapatid. 'I've been looking everywhere for you, saan ka ba nanggaling?"

"I was just.... I was just reviewing here, alam mo naman..." Then, naging malungkot ang kanyang mukha. "Kuya..."

"Oh?"

"Are you.... Have you been invited to the prom?"

"Ahh, next week na yun diba, yeah, yeah, I was..."

"Buti ka pa kuya.."

"bakit? Anong meron? May nangyari ba sa iyo?"

"Well.... Everyone knows that you're famous and..... I'm just... A freak girl that everybody knows."

"Alaina, don't say that." 

"How can I? Iyon ang katotohanan kuya, yun yung katotohanang version.... Nobody cares about me."

"But.... I care about you.."  Hinawakan ni Matt ang kamay ni Alaina, nag ring ang bell nila, ibig sabihin ay tapos na ang recess... Tumayo si Alaina at iniwan ang kanyang kapatid sa library, alam ni Matt na binu-bully sya, kahit anong gawin nya, pinapatuloy parin ng mga estudyante ang pagbubully sa kanya, he just doesn't know how to stop it...

 

Pumunta sa C.R si Alaina at tinignan ang sarili nya sa salamin, she saw herself with a glasses on her eyes, some white heads on her cheeks, "Kaya pala walang gusto ang kumausap sa akin." She took off her glasses at tinignan ang sarili nya, maya maya, biglang yumayanig ang salamin, hindi nya alam ang nangyayari ng biglang naglabas ito ng crack at nabasag.... Are you invited to the prom? If so... I want to see you there...

24. Dodgeball Attack
####################################


Pumunta sina Alaina sa gymnasium para maglaro ng Dodgeball.. Yun ang pinaka ayaw ni Alaina lalo na kapag kasama ang limang babae. The girls wore their uniform. Isan orange sando with mini shorts at mahabang medyas at sapatos, si Ms. Stephanie ang kanilang coach.

"All right everybody, pumunta na kayo sa field, the game will start." The girls started cheering dahil maglalaro na sila except kay Alaina who doesn't want to play that game at nakaupo lang sya sa bangketa at ayaw makipag cooperate. Napansin sya ni Ms. Stephanie at nilapitan sya.

"Alaina... Ba't ayaw mong sumali sa laro?" Tanong sa kanya ng guro.

"Ano po, ayaw ko pong sumali kasi.." Di kayang sabihin ni Alaina ang gagawin sa kanya ng limang babae kapag naglaro sya.

"Kasi?"

"Kasi... Masasaktan lang po ako."

"Alaina, normal lang yan sa mga taong naglalaro ng dodgeball.. Kaya tayo naglalaro nito ay para matiis ang sakit, sige na Alaina sumali ka na." Hindi naman pwedeng magsabi si ALaina ng hindi kaya tumayo na lang sya at pumunta sa gitna.

"Okay ladies, sasali si Alaina sa laro." Sabi ni Ms. Stephanie sa kanilang lahat. Ang babato, ang limang babae. Nag usap usap sila at nagtatawanan pa, alam na ni Alaina na sya ang tatamaan kaya, ihahanda nya na ang sarili nya sa larong ito.

Pumito na si Ms. Stephanie ibig sabihin, magsisimula na ang laro, inangat ni Alice bola binato buti na lang, nailagan ito ni Alaina, they moved on to the next side, binato ulit ang bola at natamaan ang isa nilang kalaro kaya na out, many were shouting and screaming habang naglalaro pero naka focus lang si Alaina sa bola.

Suddenly, the thrower formed a smile on her lips, kinuha nya ang bola at binato kay Alaina pero, nailagan nya, Alaina saw her face in disappointment, Alaina have to be careful, suddenly, tinamaan ang isang babae at na out na sya sa laro.

Many have stayed, many have not, nang mapunta na ang bola kay Alice, binato nya ito kay Alaina luckily she survived however, ang hindi nya alam, nakuha ng isang player ang bola at tinamaan si Alaina tyan ng sobrang lakas kaya napatumba sya sa sakit. Pumunta lahat ng estudyante kay Alaina at tinitignan sya.

"Alaina, Alaina? Okay ka lang ba?"

"M-ma'am, ang sakit!! Ang sobrang sakit!!" Hinawakan ni Ms. Stephanie ang tyan nya pero sumigaw ito sa sakit. Pinaalis nya ang mga estudyante at binuhat sya papunta sa clinic, Alaina is still holding her belly at ginamot sya sa clinic.

Meanwhile, habang nasa klase si Matt, tinawag sya ng principal, tungkol ito sa kanyang kapatid, Matt excused himself at pinapunta sya sa clinic, nang makarating sya doon, his face was shocked, lumapit sya kaagad sa kanyang kapatid at niyakap sya.

"Are you all right? Are you hurt?"

"Kuya... I'm fine."

"No, you're not!! Sino gumawa nito sa iyo?"

"Kuya please... Kalma ka muna."

Kumalma naman ang kanyang kuya, dumating ang principal at si Ms. Stephanie. "Good morning Matt."

"Ma'am... Ano pong nangyari sa kanya?"

"Well, recently, naaksidente sya ng bola because we were playing Dodgeball and it's my responsibility sa nangyaring trahedya."

"Sino yung kasali sa dodgeball?"

"Well, yung limang babae tapos yung kaklase nya." Napatingin sa lapag si Matt at tumingin rin sya sa kapatid nya. "Well, bibigyan namin kayo ng permission to go home early para maalagaan mo ang iyong kapatid."

"Yes ma'am." Tinulungan ni Matt si Alaina na umahon sa higaan, she is still touching her belly, inakbayan sya ni Matt at umalis sila sa eskuwelahan at pumunta sa bahay, pinahiga muna ni Matt si Alaina sa higaan at hinalikan sya sa noo. "Saglit lang baby doll, kukuha lang ako ng gamot para sa iyo."

"Salamat kuya." Ningitian lang sya at umalis sa kwarto.

 

Meanwhile sa eskuwelahan, nag papalakpakan ang mga babae dahil naging successful itong plano nila. At pinagpatuloy pa nila ang kwentuhan ang hindi nila alam.. Nakikinig ang guro sa kanila. "Kaya pala ginawa nila iyon kay Alaina."

May messsage po ako sa inyong lahat...

Everyday, nakakatanggap ako ng mga messages na ginaya ko ang Carrie, well, yun ang sabi nyo ehh, so, I revised it, pero, hindi pa rin ehh, patuloy pa rin kayo sa pagku-kumpara at pagko-comment na Carrie ito which is not entirely true, at ikaw, oo,ikaw, alam ko na nag comment ka dahil may nakita kayong reference ng Carrie pero, ba't kailangan nyo pang magalit sa akin? May ginawa ba ako sa iyo.

You can just say it to me na Kuya, mukhang nagaya nyo po yung Carrie, paki revise na lang po kasi, baka ma copyright po kayo, then okay, ni revise ko kasi madali naman akong kausap ehh, that guy PM me na ganun ang sinabi nya which is na sinunod ko, di kita kasi ma replyan kasi, baka ipagkalat mo na gaya gaya ako at walang originality, kuya o ate, tao rin ako, ilang beses ko na na violate ang 10 commandments at di ako perpekto na gumawa ng sarili kong concept.

Kaya, please lang, alam ko madami kayo mga haters at nagiisa lang ako, pero, sana naman, wag nyong ganituhin yung libro ko, ilang beses ako pinagalitan ng tatay ko at gustong gusto nyang ipatigil ang pagu-update ko tapos, ganito rin pala ang iko-comment nyo sa akin? Pinaglaban ko sa tatay ko ang librong ito.

Pasalamat nga kayo at tinutuloy ko pa ito, dapat, last month ko pa nga di ito tinuloy, kaya please lang, tumigil ka na, 15 Yrs. Old pa lang ako at madami pa akong haharaping problema okay? Ang babait ng mga introduce yourself nyo sa profile nyo...

Lahat yun, kaplastikan, oo, plastik. Ayoko na makipagawayan pa, tapos na.

29. Disturbing Video
####################################


####################################
Special Chapter: Squidward Suicide
####################################


Alam ny ba yung video na napanood nina Alice, Daniel, Matt at Alaina? I hate to say this but it's true, that video is true, nagbabasa kasi ako ng CreepyPasta ng makita ko itong video na ito, read it and watch it AT YOUR OWN RISK!!!!

 

(Full Story in CreepyPasta)

I want to start off by saying that if you want an answer at the end, prepare to be disappointed. There isn't one and I don't think there will ever be.

 

I was an intern at Nickelodeon Studios for a year back in 2005 for my degree in animation. I wasn't paid, of course, but most internships aren't. It did have some perks beyond education, though. To adults, it might not seem like a big one, but most kids at the time would have shit themselves over it.

 

Since I worked directly with the editors and animators, I got to view new episodes of cartoons days before they were aired.

 

I'll get right to the point without giving too unnecessary details. They had very recently made the Spongebob movie and the entire staff was somewhat sapped of creativity. It took them a little longer to start up the new season, sure, but the delay actually lasted longer for more upsetting reasons related to the season four premiere.

 

Two other interns and I were in the editing room along with the lead animators and sound editors for the final cut. We received the copy that was supposed to be "Fear of a Krabby Patty," and gathered around the screen to watch.

 

Now, given that everything isn't finalized at that point, animators often put up a mock title card as a joke with phony, often times lewd, titles like "How Sex Doesn't Work" instead of "Rock-a-by Bialve," the episode where Spongebob and Patrick adopt a baby Sea Scallop. There's nothing particularly funny except for a few work-related chuckles.

 

When we saw the title card "Squidward's Suicide," we didn't think it was anything more than a morbid joke. One of the interns did a small throat laugh at it. The happy-go-lucky music played as normal.

 

The story began as many of them do: Squidward was practicing his clarinet, hitting a few sour notes like usual. We hear Spongebob laughing outside and Squidward stops, yelling at him to keep it down. He mentioned something about a concert that night he needed to practice for.

 

Spongebob complies and goes to see Sandy with Patrick. The bubbles splash screen comes up and it has cut to the ending of Squidward's concert. This is where things begin to seem off, in a bad way.

 

While playing, a few frames repeat themselves and the sound doesn't. At this point, sound is synched up with the animation, so that isn't very common. When he stops playing, the sound finishes as if the skip never happened, too. There's a slight murmuring in the crowd before everyone begins to boo him.

 

This wasn't the normal cartoon booing that's common in the show. You could clearly hear malice in it. Squidward was in full frama nd looked visibly afraid. The shot cut to the crowd, with Spongebob in center frame. He, too, is booing. It was very much unlike him. However, that wasn't the oddest thing.

 

The oddest thing was that everyone had hyper-realistic eyes. They were very detailed. They weren't shots of real people's eyes, but something a bit more real than CGI. The pupils were red, too. Some of us looked at each other, obviously confused, but since we weren't the writers we didn't question its appeal to children...yet.

 

The shot cuts to Squidward as he sat on the edge of his bed, looking forlorn. The view out of his porthole window was of a night sky, so it probably wasn't very long after the concert.

 

At this point, there was no sound. There was LITERALLY no sound. There wasn't even feedback from the speakers in the room. It was as if the speakers were turned off, though their status showed them working perfectly.

 

Squidward simply sat there, blinking, in this silence for about thirty seconds until he began to sof softly. He put his tentacles over his eyes and cried quietly for a full minute more, all the while a sound in the background slowly growing from nothing to barely audible. It sounded like a slight breeze through a forest.

 

The screen slowly began to zoom in on his face. By slowly, I mean it was only noticeable if you look at shots ten seconds apart side by side. His sobbing got louder and louder, more full of hurt and anger.

 

The screen twitched for a split second, as if it twisted in on itself, before returning to normal. The wind-through-the-trees sound slowly got louder and louder - more severe, too - as if a storm was brewing somewhere.

 

The eerie part was that this sound and Squidward's sobbing sounded real. It was as if the sound wasn't coming from the speakers, but as if the speakers were holes the sound was coming through from the other side. As good quality as the studio likes to have, they don't purchase the equipment to be good enough to produce sound of that quality.

 

Below the sound of the wind and sobbing was something that sounded like faint laughing. It came at odd intervals and never lasted more than a second, so you had a hard time pinning it. After 30 seconds of this, the screen blurred and twitched vilently as something flashed over the screen like a subliminal image.

 

The lead animation editor paused and rewound frame by frame. What was saw was horrible.

 

It was a still photo of a dead child. He couldn't have been more than six years old. His face was mangled and bloodied. One eye was popped out and dnagling over his upturned face. he was naked, down to his underwear, and his stomach was crudely cut open with his entrails lying beside him.

 

He was lying on some pavement. The most upsetting part was there was the shadow of the photographer visible. There was no cripe tape, no evidence bags or markers, and the angle was completely off for a shot designed to be evidence. It would seem the photographer was the person responsible for the child's death.

 

We were, of course, mortified. However, we pressed on, hoping it was just a sick joke. The screen flipped back to Squidward, still sobing. He was louder than before and only half of his body was in the frame. There was no what appeared to be blood running down his face from his eyes.

 

The blood was also done in a hyper-realistic style. It looked as if you touched it, you'd get blood on your fingers. The wind sounded as if it were a gale blowing through a forest. There were even snapping sounds of branches.

 

The laughing, a deep baritone, lasted longer and came more frequently. After about twenty seconds, the screen again twisted and showed another single-frame photo.

 

The editor was reluctant to go back, as we all were, but we knew he had to. This time, the photo was that of what appeared a little girl no older than the first child. She was lying on her stomach, her barrettes in a pool of blood next to her. Her left eye, too, was popped out and she was naked except for underpants. Her entrails were piled on top of her above a crude cut along her back.

 

Again, the body on the street and the photographer's shadow was visible. It was very similar in shape and size to the first. I had to choke back vomit and one intern, the only female in the room, ran out.

 

The show resumed. About five seconds after this second photo, all sound stopped like it was when this scene started. Squidward put his tentacles down and his eyes were done in a hyper-realistic style like the others in the beginning of the episode.

 

They were bleeding, bloodshot and pulsating. He stared at the screen, as if watching the viewer. After ten seconds, he started sobbing. This time, he wasn't covering his eyes at all.

 

The sound was piercing and loud. The most fear-inducing part of all of this was his sobbing. It was mixed in with screams. Tears and blood were dripping down Squidward's face at a heavy rate.

 

The wind sound came back and so did the deep-voiced laughing. The next still photo lasted for a good five frames. The animator was able to stop it on the fourth and backed up.

 

This time, the photo was of a boy about the same age as other children, but the scene was different. The entrails were just being pulled out from a stomach wound by a large hand. The boy's right eye was popped and dangling with blood trickling down it. The animator proceeded. The next was different, though we couldn't tell how.

 

He went to the next after that, and it was the same thing. He went back to the first and played them quicker. I lost it, vomiting on the floor. The animating and sound editors were gasping at the screen.

 

The file frames were not as if they were five different photos. They were played out as if they were frames from a video. We saw the hand slowly lift out the guts, we saw the kid's eyes focus on it, and we even saw two frames of him beginning to blink.

 

The lead sound editor told us to stop. He had to call in the creator to see it. Mr. Hillenburg arrived within fifteen minutes. He was confused as to why he was called down there, so the editor continued the episode.

 

Once the few frames were shown, all sound again stopped. Squidward was staring at the viewer, his entire face in the frame, for about three seconds. The shot quickly panned out and that deep voice said, "DO IT." The next thing we see is a shotgun in Squidward's hands.

 

He immediately puts the gun in his mouth and pulls the trigger. Realistic blood and brain matter splattered the wall and bed behind him. He flies back from the force. The last five seconds of the episode show his body on the bed, on his side, with one eye dangling on what's left of his head above the floor, staring blankly at it. The episode ends there.

 

Mr. Hillenburg was obviously angry about it. He demanded to know what the hell was going on. Most people left the room at that point, so it was just a handful of us to watch it again. Viewing the episode twice only served to imprint the entirety of it into my mind and caused me horrible nightmares. I'm sorry I stayed.

 

The only theory we could think of was that someone in the chain from the drawing studio to here edited the file. The CTO was called into analyze when it happened. The analysis of the file did show it was edited over by new material.

 

However, the timestamp of it happening was a mere 24 seconds before we began viewing it. All equipment involved was examined for foreign software and hardware, as well as glitches - as if the time stamp may have glitched and showed the wrong time - but everything checked out fine.

 

We don't know what happened and, to this day, nobody does. There was a police investigation due to the nature of the photos, but nothing came of it. No child seen was identified and no clues were gathered from the data involved or physical clues in the photos.

 

I never believed in unexplainable phenomena before, but now that I've seen it for myself...if something happens and I can't prove anything about it beyond anecdotal evidence, I think twice about things.

32. Psychopath's Game.
####################################


Isang kakaibang uri ng laro ang lumabas sa computer screen, isang laro na ang ang Title Sonic.Exe. "Sonic? Alaina, let me play the game, alam ko itong laro na ito."

"Okay." Pinindot ni Matt ang enter button at, biglang nagbago ang itsura ng title screen, the screen went to the 3 characters, isang character lang at ito si Tails, they found out that the background sound ng game is somehow, reversed pero, the weird thing is, nagpatuloy lang sila sa paglalaro, lumitaw na si tails sa game, the only controls were, left and right, Matt clicked the right button at tumakbo si Tails to the right, habang tumatakbo sya, the reversed 16bit song is getting louder and louder, making their hearts beats like hell.

Habang tumatakbo si Tails sa right side ng map, they saw an animals body lying on the floor, it was horrible at mayroon pang mga piles ng dead body ng mga animals then, the music stops, pero, patuloy parin sa pagtatakbo si tails ng biglang nakita nila ang isang itsura ni Sonic pero, his eyes were bloodshot, bloody mouth and a devilish smile, Tails walked in fornt of him at walang hinahawakan na button si Matt then, the screen went black pero, naglabas ito ng isang black and white na message.

Gusto mo bang maglaro? Kung ganun, dapat mabilis ka dahil, kapag hindi, mahuhuli kita.

Nagiba ang itsura ng settings, this time, nasa hell version na si Tails ng Hills, Matt clicked the left button ng biglang nakita ni Matt si Tails, he quickly clicked the right side at ngayon, hinahabol habol sya ni Sonic, they are now intensed and scared dahil mabilis ang takbo ni Sonic maya maya, he touched Tails at umiyak lang sya.... For like 5 minutes, then, Sonic appeared out of nowhere, the screen went black, at may narinig silang sigaw na ikinagulat nila, pagkatapos, lumitaw ang isang message.

You're too slow..

Bumalik ulit sa character selection, tapos na si tails at ang sumunod, si Knuckles, kinlick ito ni Matt at may narinig silang demonyong tawa. Lumabas ang itsura ni Knuckles, the background is somehow disturbing, tumakbo sa right side si Knuckles, he kept on running habang ang music ay nagiging intense and disturbing, maya maya, biglang sumulpot ang Demon version na Sonic at nagblack yung screen...

Lumitaw ulit si Knuckles, this time, yung floors nito ay maraming dugo at masyado na itong disturbing, maya maya, biglang lumitaw si Sonic sa likod ni Knuckles then.... 

The screen went black... At nakarinig ulit sila ng sigaw.... And another message has appeared.

You're way too slow

"Kuya, I don't want to play that game." Maiyak-iyak na sabi ni Alaina.

"Okay, iiwanan na lang natin ito and babalik na lang tayo sa room."

"Okay." Lumabas sila ng Classroom at pumunta sa medyo madilim na hallway pero, may ilaw pa... Maya maya, biglang namatay ang ilaw... Matt took the flashlight, may nairinig silang unusual noise, biglang may nalaglag na gamit sa gilid nila, tinutukan iyon ni Matt pero, wala doon, may dumating sa right side nila, pero, wala silang nakita...

(Open the Multimedia.... Listen at your own risk.)

Go to sleep, my baby....

Tomorrow is another day...

Go to sleep, my baby...

Narinig nila Matt at Alaina ang kantang iyon, Matt slowly, turn his flashlight on his back.. When suddenly..

"BOO!!" Isang lalaking ulay puti ang balat nito, kakaibang uri ng mata at may dugo ito sa bibig nya, napasigaw sina Alaina at Matt sa kanya, dali dali silang tumakbo, then, nagtago sila sa isang sulok.. "Hahaha.... Both of you should go to sleep, gabi na mga bata, dapat natutulog na kayo sa inyong mga kwarto, hahahehahaheha!!" Sabi ng isang baliw na lalaki.

"Kuya... Who is that guy?"

"Di ko sya kilala Alaina pero, dapat tumakhimik muna tayo, baka makita nya tayo." Nakita nila ang paa ng baliw na binata, his foot is slowly walking then... Huminto sya, pumikit si Alaina at niyakap sya ni Matt then, nagpatuloy lang sa paglalakad ang baliw until mawala na sya... Slowly na tumayo sina Matt at Alaina when suddenly, isang manika na naglalakad ang nakakita sa kanilang dalawa.

Ito yung manika na parati nilang nakikita sa t.v "You should go to sleep." Sabi ng manika, pagtalikod nila, nandoon ang baliw na lalaki na nakangiti ng nakakatakot. May dala dala syang kutsilyo at sasaksakin nya na si Alaina pero, tinulak sya ni Matt. 

"Run Alaina, get out of here."

"Pero kuya."

Napaupo sa lapag at napasandal sa pintuan si Alaina.

"Kuya... Please save me.."

Meanwhile, habang umiiyak at nakatakpan ang mukha ni Alaina sa kanyang mga palad, narinig nya ang pangalan nya mula sa boses ng isang lalaki, she opened the door, at nakita nya ang kanyang kuya na hinahanap sya, she ran to him at niyakap sya.

"Kuya, I thought namatay ka na."

Find the 8 pages around the room, be careful, someone is going to follow you, be watchful and careful.

They took the first page na nakalagay sa lamesa, the drawing seems different, lumabas sila sa room at naglakad sa madilim na hallway, kinuha ni Matt ang flashlight at tinutok sa harapan nila, naglakad sila sa hallway ng makita nila ang ikalawang page. just like the first page, kakaiba ang drawing, some sort of pattern, they took it at may narinig silang padyak ng paa sa kanilang likuran, tinutok ni Matt ang flashlight pero, wala silang nakita.

"Kuya, sa tingin mo ba... Sila ulit iyon?"

"I think so Alaina, pero, we have to be very careful." Nagpatuloy sila sa paglalakad, habang naglalakad, may narinig silang kakaibang tawa. It's the same laugh they heard last minute ago, tumingin sila sa likod pero, waa naman doon, nagpatuloy ulit sila sa paglalakad ng biglang napatili si Alaina dahil..

Nakita nya ang Psychopath malapit sa pader, tinutok doon ni Matt ang flashlight pero, wala silang nakita.

"Alaina, are you sure may nakita ka?"

Pagharap nila, nakita nila ang lalaki na kulay pula ang mata, nakatingin sa kanila, may dala dala syang chainsaw, binuksan nya ito at nag iikot na ang mga blades. Tumakbo sila kaagad paalis sa kanya, pero, hinahabol sila ng lalaki.

Nakakita ng pinuan si Alaina, hinila nya ang kanyang kuya papasok sa maliit na kwarto, tumahimik silang dalawa, naririnig nila ang padyak ng lalaki, hanggang sa nawala na ito, pagharap ulit nila, nakita nila ang papel na may drawing, they took it at lumabas ulit sa kwarto, tumakbo sila sa hallway paakyat sa hagdanan ng biglang nakita nila ang lalaki na may hawak ng chainsaw, nakatingin sa kanila.

The psycho turned on his chainsaw at naglakad pababa sa hagdanan.

Palapit na ng palapit silang dalawa kay Matt at Alaina ng biglang lumabas ang mga apoy sa pader, inangat ng lalaking kulay pula ang mga mata ang kanyang chainsaws ng biglang sumabog ang mga pader, natumba ang lalaki, tumayo kaagad ang magkapatid at umalis sa Fire Exit at tumakbo sa madilim na hallway, maya maya, sinusundan sila ng apoy, mabilis na tumakbo silang dalawa sa hallway ng biglang napansin nila ang apat na pages na nakadikit sa bulletin board, they took it at may 6 na silang pages.. 

They keep on running until nakapasok sila sa isang classroom na punong puno ng mga drawing, this is the same thing they saw sa isang classroom, pero, that drawer is referring to a man named Death.. They saw the date of the Death's birthday... June 6th, 1966 or known as 06/06/66.

He will create a test for this people dahil, tinadhana talaga silang patayin pero, they cheated him, that's why..  He will do everything to kill them."

"Do you think... Itong taong ito ay tinadhanang mamatay?"

"I think so... Hey kuya, nandoon yung dalawang pages." Kinuha iyon kaagad ni Matt at kumpleto na ang papel nila, tumakbo sila diretso sa Math Department, they attached all the eight pages sa frame at naglabas....

Isang uri ng symbolo na kung saan, nandoon ang bungo na mukha a may hawak syang Scythe... Then suddenly, nagbukas ang pader at nakita nila si Nina na nakatali ang buong katawan sa lamesa at nandoon sa ibabaw ang Swinging axe, they only got one minute left, they have to find the four keys sa loob ng kwarto pero, wala silang makita.

Pinagpapawisan at hindi na nila alam ang gagawin nilang dalawa, maya maya, they only got 10 seconds left at bumababa na ang swinging axe... Ng biglang, dumapo ito sa katawan ni Nina at nahati ito sa dalawa, nanlaki ang mga mata nilang dalawa at biglang bumukas ang t.v sa gilid, ang lumabas, isang lalaki na naka shades at spiky ang buhok.

"You see.... I'm special, I'm a kind of human who has... Well, let's say, something powerful... Ngayon, everytime na mangyayari ang Death Test, makikielam ako, I will do everything para lang magawa nyo ang quest na ipabibigay sa inyo ng mga Proxies ko."

If you're interested to investigate, go to the library at makikita nyo ang mini quest nyo doon." Then, nawala ang lalaki sa t.v screen, napaupo na lang silang dalawa sa lapag.

36. Long Lost Friend
####################################


Nagising si Alaina sa clinic at nakita nya ang kanyang kuya na nagre-recover na sa kanyang sugat, nakita nya rin si Anna na nagpapahinga at nakasandal ang ulo nito sa lamesa. Napatayo si Alaina sa upuan at tumingin sa bintana, she didn't saw any police car or ambulance o kaya'y mga media. Nothing, wala. She looked at the time and it's 3:20 AM.

Naisipan nya na mag investigate muli, tinanggal nya ang mga harang sa pintuan, she slowly opened the door at madilim parin ang hallway, kinuha nya ang flashlight ng kanyang kuya at naglakad papunta sa library.

------ Library ------

Nang makapasok sya sa loob ng library, hinanap nya ang isang libro, ang Unsolved Case. Nang makita nya iyon, kinuha nya at nilapag sa lamesa. Binuksan nya ang table of contents at may nakita syang case that caught her interest. Case #66: Blackholm Mansion. Binuklat nya yung case 66 at nakita nya ang isang mansion na before and after, yung before nya, medyo luma at maayos ang mansion pero yung ngayon, sunog at sira sira.

Ito yung nakasulat. On January 16, 1998, isang pamilya ang lumipat sa Blackholm Mansion para sa kanilang business enterprise, this family contains 5 members, at ang bunso, Si Jeffrey Anderson. Nanlaki ang mga mata ni Alaina ng malaman nya na si Jeffrey Anderson ang kasama sa Blackholm Incident. Pinagpatuloy nya parin ang pagbabasa.

Si Jeffrey Anderson ay nagaral sa Orlean Academy however, sya ay binubully ng mga tao at ang mga nakapaligid sa kanya, one day, his family's business went bankrupt at mas lalo sila naging mahirap sa buhay.

One day, Jeffrey was invited to a slumber party with a FAKE invitation card, nang pagpasok nya daw doon sa loob, he was being pranked by everyone, in 1:06 AM, nakita nila si Jeffrey na nasusunog in unknown reason.

Doctors said that the burnts na nanggaling sa katawan ni Jeffrey resulted 3rd degree burn at namuti ang balat nito, but, the strangest thing is that gustong gusto ni Jeffrey ang kanyang kulay, he even cutted his own eyelids para hindi sya pumikit, suddenly, 

On January 18, 1998, their mansion was burned, killing every family member except Jeffrey Anderson, people said they no longer saw the boy and now... Criminologist at ang mga Private investigator were no longer solving this case dahil sa kakulangan ng evidence at mga witness and because of this, Case #66 was never been solved.

Sinara ni Alaina ang libro na gulat na gulat, he knew that boy, the boy which Alaina save him from harm.

"Jeffrey, bakit ka laging magisa dito sa playground?"

"Nobody wants to be with me, they think i'm weird."

"Jeffrey, thats bad, kung iyon ang iniisip sa iyo sa akin, hindi."

"Really?"

"Yeah, what friends are we for? If anything happens to you, ako ang magbabantay sa iyo."

"But... you're a girl."

"Jeffrey, I'm a lot stronger than you think I am." Tapos ngumiti sya sa akin.

------ January 16, 1998 ------

"Alaina... This is the last time you will see me here sa playground."

"bakit?"

"Kasi... Lilipat na kami sa isang mansyon."

"Then... I will never going to see you again here."

"That's okay." May binigay sya sa akin ng isang bracelet na gawa sa glitters at diamonds. "Wow, thank you Jeffrey."

"As long as you have this in your hand... Hindi mo ko makakalimutan and I too will never forget you." At nagyakapan kami.

 

Sa buong buhay ni Alaina, isang tao ang gustong pumatay sa kanya... Isang kaibigan na pinagkatiwalaan nya ay may tangkang patayin sya. "I can't believe it... Jeffrey.. Is actually my long lost friend." Tumayo sya sa kanyang upuan at tumakbo papunta sa Class 3-C Humility. When she reached that classroom, as usual may mga drawings ito at kung ano ano pa. Pumunta sya sa isang desk na may Yearbook ng Orlean Academy. "How did this thing get here?" Sabi ni Alaina sa kanyang isip.

She opened at nakita nya si Jeffrey sa picture. She knew it... Nung una nyang ma encounter yung lalaking nagsasabi ng Go to Sleep ay kahawig ng kanyang kaibigan na si Jeffrey. "I knew that someday you will know who really I am." Isang seryosong boses ang narinig ni Alaina sa kanyang likuran.

"J-jeff.." 

 

Nagising si Matt at si Anna ng makita nila na wala na si Alaina. Tumunog ang bell at may nagsalita sa speaker. "Now... Ipagsasama ko na ang 4th at ang 5th test... Go to the Gymnasium at makikita nyo na ang susunod na biktima." At nawala ang boses.

"Anna. Where's Alaina? Alalang tanong ni Matt sa kanya.

"I don't know where she went." 

"Fuck... Alaina, please, sana wag kang susunod, please don't take her next. Please don't take her next." 

At maya maya, biglang lumabas ang mga luha sa mata ni Matt.

37. Tug-Of-Death
####################################


"J-jeff." 

"Now that you knew about me..." Napahinto lang sya ng saglit, tumingin sa likod si Alaina and he saw him, white pale color with a chelsea smile on his face. Seeing him made her scared and pity at the same time. "What are you going to do with me?" Tanong sa kanya ni Alaina.

"I was goin to ask you the same question."

"Why Jeff.... Why be like this?"

"Hindi mo naiintindihan ang lahat Alaina, you don't understand everything."

"Then tell me... At iintindihin ko ang nararamdaman mo."

"You have to go."

"No... I'm not going hangga't hindi mo sa akin sinasabi ang dahilan mo kung bakit ka naging psychopath."

"Please Alaina... Just.. Just go, I don't want to hurt you."

"Jeff, ano ba ang kinatatakutan mo?" Biglang tumaas ang tono ni Alaina sa kanya.

"Enough Alaina." Nanginginig na sabi ni Jeff kay Alaina.

"No why? Why did you turned to this? Why did you turn yourself into a monster?!"

"I SAID ENOUGH!!" Nakataas na ang kanyang kamay na may kutsilyo at natakot sa kanya si Alaina. "Don't you see.... I'm a killer, I kill everything!!"

"Including... Me?" Nakita nya na tumingin sa lapag si Jeff. Hahawakan na sana sya ni Alaina pero, parang napaso yung kanyang kamay. "You have to go, nagsisimula na ang 4th at ang 5th test." At umalis lang ang binata palabas sa classroom. "Jeff.... I don't know the reason why you're like this... We've trusted each other for like 4 Months, Jeff.... Why?" Lumabas na lang sya ng classroom at bumalik ulit sa clinic.

Nang makarating sya doon, nakita sya kaagad ng kanyang kuya bago pa ito buksan yung pinto, tumakbo kaagad si Matt kaagad kay Alaina at niyakap ang dalaga kaagad. "Alaina, saan ka ba nanggaling? Hinahanap kita rito? Shit Alaina, don't do this again."

"I'm sorry kuya, I was just.... I was just investigating."

"Kailangan na nating pumunta sa gymnasium... Ang biktima ay si Alice." Tumakbo kaagad silang tatlo papunta sa gym.. nang makarating na kaagad sila doon, nakita nila ang dalawang dalaga na nakadena an kamay nito, sinubukan ni Alice na hilahin ang isang kamay pero, yung isang babae, nahila rin yung kamay, it's more like Tug-Of-War. Maya maya, biglang may nagsalita sa speaker.

"My my... What a pleasant surprise.... How do you like my trap? Is it beautiful? Or is it.... Violent? I call this trap, Tug-Of-Death, it's all bout pull.... Pag nahila ng isang tao ang kanyang kaliwang kamay, mahihila ang kaliwang kamay ng taong nasa harapan nya... Para bang.. May tali yung bawat joints nila... If someone pulled out their bodies, the other one will do the same... So... Anong mangyayari sa kanila? Ganito, after the 2 minute preparation, lalabas ang spinning blade sa kanilang likuran... In order to escape that trap, isa sa kanila ang pwedeng mamatay... Either the left side or the right side... Oh yeah... Kayong tatlo, sit down and enjoy the show... Goodluck."

Nawala na yung boses sa speaker. Tumakbo silang tatlo kaagad kay Alice. Alice is crying so hard that she didn't even want this, at niyakap sya kaagad ni Alice. "Alaina."

"Alice... It's okay we're here..."

"Alaina, I don't want this, bakit nangyayari ito? Why is this happening?"

"Hindi ko alam ang reason but please Alice... Promise me, promise me that you will survive this trap."

"How, what will I do? I rather die than killing people."

"We have no other choice but to kill, it's your choice, either kill your friend, or die.." Tumingin sa lapag si Alice, then, she looked at Alaina with a different smile... A kind of smile that made Alaina's skin go up. Isang uri ng ngiti na gutom na gutom sa dugo at karahasan. "Thank you Alaina... I've been waiting for all this years."

Tumunog ang bell ibig sabihin, tapos na ang 2 minute preparation, maya maya, biglang may nagsalita sa speaker. "Okay.... Kayong tatlo, umupo na kayo sa bangketa and watch the show... Participants, get ready..." Biglang bumukas ang projector at nandoon ang timer..

10....9....8....7..

Biglang lumitaw ang mga spinning blades sa kanilang likuran pero di pa ito umiikot..

6...5...4..

Their hearts were racing to the beat, thinking what will happen next.

3...2..

Sweats are now coming on their faces..

1.. BOOM

Hinila ni Alice ang kanyang kaliwang kamay pero, hinihila rin ng isang babae yung kanyang kamay kaya, pwersa laban sa pwersa silang dalawa, napasigaw sa lakas si Alice kaya, hinila nya ang buong katawan nya, napansin ng babae nahihila sya papunta sa blade kaya, hinila nya rin ang kanyang sarili.

"Alice please, don't give up... You can do this." Maya maya, tumawa si Alice. "You know what... This is so much fun, I never knew that this could be fun." Tapos, nilakasan nya pa ang sarili nya na ihila ang sarili at kitang kita sa itsura ng babae na nahihirapan na syang hilahin ang kanyang sarili..

Few inches left na lang sa babae at masha-shattered sya into pieces. Pero, hindi nagpatalo ang dalaga, nilakasan nya ang hila at nagulat si Alice, at nasugatan yung kanyang kaliwang paa. Napasinghap sa hangin si Alice.

Naging kamao na ang mga kamay ni Alice and forces herself to pull her body.. Ibang Alice na ang nakikita nilang tatlo... This Alice is somehow... Different from the Alice they knew.. Alaina thought that.... The reason ay nangyayari ang Death Test sa kanilang school... Is to train them how to kill a person.

Maya maya, they saw the girl being shattered into pieces including the internal organs, nagulat ang tatlo at tinakpan ang sariling mukha dahil sa matinding pananaw. They heard Alice's devilish laugh. maya maya, natanggal ang kadena nito sa buong katawan nya, ang tatlo hindi makapalapit kay Alice.

"Oh? Bakit di kayo makalapit?" Inosenteng tanong sa kanila ni Alice, parang nanlamig ang mga paa nila at hindi na sila makagalaw.

"Kung ganyan kayo ngayon sa akin? I have no other choice." Pumunta sya sa bandang area na kung saan nandoon ang fire emergency equipments, binasag nya ang salamin gamit ang kanyang ulo at kinuha ang ax. Nanlaki ang kanilang mga mata at nagtakbuhan paalis sa Gym at ngayon nasa madilim sila na parte ng Hallway.

"HAHAHAHAHAHA" Isang demonyong tawa ang kanilang narinig maya maya, narinig din nila ang tunog ng isang malaking gunting, nakita nila na parating na ang lalaking kulay pula ang mata, napatingin sila sa likod at nakita rin nila si Alice na nakangiti rin sa kanila.

Nacornered silang tatlo, nalaman ni Alaina na wala si Jeff, papalapit na ang dalawa sa kanila ng biglang nabutas ang lapag at nalaglag silang tatlo, natamaan ang ulo ni Anna at namatay sya... Hindi makatayo ang dalawang magkapatid dahil sa lakas ng impact ng pagbagsak nila.

Blur ang vision ni Alaina, nakita nya ang isang lalaki na kulay puti ang balat at tinignan sya. "T-tulungan mo ko.." Isang bulong ni Alaina sa lalaki pero, di sya tinulungan.

"I'm sorry Alaina." Maya maya, nandilim ang paningin nya....

(To Be continued)

38. Childhood Memories
